diakrinetai kai kathairetai kai pollois eterois anamignutai kai merizetai pollakhe kai pante pheretai kai khronizei kat ouden ton morion oti d eiper emene drimu pantos an elkose kai ta entos ek ton automaton elkon epignose gignetai gar pollois pollakis tois men ex edesmaton mokhtheron tois d ek tinos en auto to somati diaphthoras kai sepedonos e kaloumene kakokhumia kai toutois eniote men elkoutai ti kai ton entos os ta polla de to ten phusin apotribesthai ta kata ten exin perittomata pros to derma touth elkoutai pollois kai sunekhesin elkesi karkinos te gar kai phagedaina kai erpes o anabibroskomenos anthrakes te kai ta kheironeia kai telepheia kaloumena kai allai muriai geneseis elkon ekgonoi tes toiautes eisi kakokhumias out oun ton toiouton ouden aporon oute dia ti ton pharmakon enia men ouden emas exothen adikounta mega ti kakon ergazetai katapothenta tina de pollakis men eblapsen eiso lephthenta pollakis d ophelesen enia d ou monon esothen alla kai exothen adikei sullebden d eipein ouden omoios esothen te kai exothen energein pephuken oute gar o tou luttontos kunos aphros outh o tes aspidos outh o tes ekhidnes ios oi de kai khoris elkous exothen prospesontes adikein pepisteuntai ten isen ekhousi dunamin e to dermati monon omilesantes e eiso metalephthentes ou men oud ekeino thaumazein axion ei tinon pharmakon ouk exikneitai pros to bathos e dunamis ou gar anagkaion apanta ten auten ekhein iskhun ei de polla ton eiso lambanomenon en men tode to kairo kai meta tosesde posotetos kai tes pros tade mixeos ophelesen akairos de kai polla kai amikta lephthenta blaben enegken ouden oud enteuthen aporema to logo kai gar kai tois sitiois uparkhei touto ge kai to puri kai pasin os outo phanai tois prospiptousi to somati summetrou goun phlogos estin ote deometha kai khromenoi megalos pros autes oninametha kaitoi tes ametrou kaiouses emas outo de kai psukhrou posis e men summetros oninesin e d ametros eskhatos blaptei ti toinun thaumaston einai ti pharmakon outo dunamei thermon os ei men polu te lambanoito kai keno to somati prospheroito diabibroskein te kai katakaiein auto ei de pantelos oligon eie e kai sun tois kolazousi ten iskhun autou pros to blaptein meden eti kai thermainon ophelein opon goun etoi ton kurenaikon e ton medikon e ton parthikon auton kath eauton ouk enestin alupos labein all ei pantelos oligos e sun allois en kairo prosekonti lephtheie megalos ophelei tauti men oun osa thermainei to soma metaboles arkhen en auto labonta kathoti prosthen errethe palin antithermainein auto pephuken osa de psukhei kathaper opos mekonos ou metaballetai pros tou somatos oud ep oligon all euthus auto nika kai metaballei kan ei thermenas auta doies esti gar e sphon auton phusis psukhra kathoti kai to udor orthos oun kai touto sun pollois allois up aristotelous eiretai to ton thermon kai psukhron kai xeron kai ugron somaton ta men einai kath eauta toiauta ta de kata sumbebekos oion kai to udor kath eauto men psukhron kata sumbebekos de pote kai thermon all e men epiktetos autou thermasia takheos apollutai menei d e sumphutos psukhrotes os oun udor thermon epiblethen phlogi katasbennusin auten outo kai to mekonion ei kai oti malista thermenas doies apopsuxeis te ten en to zoo thermasian kai kindunon epaxeis thanatou pant oun ta toiauta pharmaka brakhea te didomena kai sun tois kolazein auton to sphodron tes psuxeos dunamenois estin ote khreian tina parekhei tois somasin emon os en tois peri pharmakon eiresetai kai gar de kai to dia ton kantharidon pharmakon ikanos oninesi tous uderikous kaitoi toupipan elkoi ten kustin e kantharis all epeidan upo te ton mikhthenton aute kolasthe kai somati prosagetai pampollen ugroteta periekhontai kenoi dia ton ouron auto malist oun khre prosekhein ton noun en apasi tois dunamei thermois e psukhrois einai legomenois eite tes phuseos esti ton trephein dunamenon eite monen aphormen alloioseos lambanonta kapeita kata ten oikeian phusin alloioumena diatithesi pos to soma kai triton epi toutois ei med olos alloioutai pros autou kata meden ei men gar ek tou genous eie ton trephonton ei men kratetheie thermainei me kratethenta de psukhei ei de ton ep oligon poson alloioumenon thermainei mainei pantos ei de ton med olos psukhei malista prosekhein d os eiretai malista kai diorizesthai ta kath eauta ton kata sumbebekos ouk epi thermon kai psukhron monon all ouden etton auton eph ugron te kai xeron enia gar ton toiouton xera tais ousiais uparkhonta pollo thermo takenta phantasian ugrotetos elaben os khalkos kai sideros e kath eauta men estin ugra kathaper o krustallos akrato de psuxei plesiasanta xera phainetai khre toinun apanton touton ten krisin oukh aplos poieisthai kathoti kan tois emprosthen elegomen alla meta tou sunepiskeptesthai pos ekhei thermotetos e psukhrotetos ei men gar oliges metekhonta thermotetos omos ugra phainoito dia ten oikeian phusin esti toiauta kan ei meta dapsilous thermasias xera ta d etoi reonta meta thermotetos zeouses e pepegota dia psuxin akraton ou kath eauta nomizein einai ta men ugra ta de xera taute t oun diaireisthai ta kath eauta ton kata sumbebekos anapheronta te pros auta tauta ten krisin outo poieisthai ton dunamei thermon e psukhron e xeron e ugron ou gar pros to kata sumbebekos alla pros to kath eauto krinesthai khre to dunamei koine d epi panton e krisis kai mia to takhos tes alloioseos omonumos de legomenou tou thermou kai psukhrou kai xerou kai ugrou to men gar kat epikratesin outos onomazetai to d os akran ekhon es paronomazetai poioteta eis opoteron an auton etoimos methistetai to krinomenon estai dunamei toiouton elaion goun esti dunamei thermon oti radios phlox gignetai kata tauta de kai retine kai pitta kai asphaltos oinos de dioti radios aima gignetai kata tauta de kai meli kai kreas kai gala tauti men oun olais alloioumena tais ousiais trophai ton alloiounton eisi ta de kata mian entinoun poioteta ten alloiosin iskhonta te kai parekhonta pharmaka monon osper ge kai osa tais olais eauton ousiais atrepta menonta diatithesi pos to soma pharmaka men esti kai tauta khalepa de kai phthartika tes tou zoou phuseos othenper oimai to genos auton apan onomazetai deleterion ou gar de dia touto ge lekteon ouk einai to genei deleteria ta toiauta dioti pantelos elakhista prosakhthenta blaben oudemian aistheten epipherei outo gar an oude to pur eie thermon oud e khion psukhra os kai touton ge ta pantapasi smikra saphes ouden apotelei peri tois somasin emon pathos spintheros gar enos ekatoston meros esti men pantos to genei pur all ou monon ouk an emas kauseien e thermeneien all oud an aisthesin tina paraskhoi prospeson outo de kai to tes psukhras ranidos ekatoston meros ou monon ouden an blapseien e psuxeien all oud an aisthesin tina paraskhoi me toinun outo mede ta deleteria krinein alla te tes oles phuseos enantiosei ten d enantiosin ek tes en meso krinein metaboles oion eutheos apo ton stoikheion outh udor eis pur oute pur eis udor metaballein pephuken all eis aera men ampho ekeinos d eis ekatera eis allela de taut oudamos amesos men oun e eis aera metabole tou udatos osautos de kai tou puros ouk amesos d e puros kai udatos eis allela taut oun allelois estin enantia kai polemia kata de ton auton tropon kai opos mekonos anthropeio somati teleos estin enantios ouden eis auton oute kata mian poioteta drasai dunameno oute polu de mallon eti kath olen ten ousian en men de to genos touto ton deleterion eteron de ton aphormen men tina metaboles lambanonton ek tes en emin thermasias eis polueideis d enteuthen ektrepomenon alloioseis uph on diaphtheiresthai ten phusin emon sumbebeke panta gar ta toiauta to genei deleteria kan dia smikroteta pote meden aistheton apergazetai ta men de diabibroskonta kai seponta kai tekonta ten tou somatos emon phusin eikotos onomazetai dunamei therma ta d au psukhonta kai nekrounta psukhra ta men oun protera paralogon ouden out auta paskhein oute tois somasin emon enapergazesthai dokei thermo gar somati plesiasanta kai tina ropen alloioseos enteuthen labonta ta men eis eskhaten aphikneitai thermoteta ta d eis sepedona diatithesin oun eikotos kai ta ton zoon somata kata ten eauton diathesin osa de psukhei to soma kan thermenas auta prosenegkes aporian ou smikran epipherei tinos pote phuseos estin ei gar apax energeia therma gegone ti ou thermainei to zoon e ei mepo tethermantai pos phainetai therma lusis de tes aporias ei dioristheie to kath auto psukhron tou kata sumbebekos os aristoteles edidaxen apollutai gar en takhei ton kata sumbebekos thermon e epiktetos diathesis ost eis ten arkhaian auta phusin epanerkhesthai radios en de to plesiazein emin ta phusei men psukhra kata sumbebekos de therma duo taut ex anagkes gignetai to men epikteton auton apollutai thermon e d oikeia krasis ouden upo tes emeteras paskhousa menei psukhra kai ti thaumaston ei mekonos opos e mandragoras e koneion e ti ton toiouton ei kai thermanthenta prosenekhtheie mikron usteron gignetai psukhra ptisanes kai galaktos kai khondrou kai artou tauton toutois paskhonton epeidan eis arroston empesonta gastera me kratethe pros autes emeitai goun pollakis ikanos psukhra kai to ge toutou meizon o de kai ippokrates epesemenato kaitoi khumos on ede to phlegma kak ton sition ton me pephthenton en te gastri gennomenon omos psukhron aptomenois phainetai ou monon en te gastri sustan alla kak ton phlebon auton upo tinos ton kathaironton pharmakon elkhthen kaitoi ge gliskhrotaton esti phusei kai biaios agetai all omos oud e bia tes olkes ekthermainein auto dunatai ti oun thaumaston ei kai to mekonion outos enantion emon te phusei pharmakon apopsukhetai men autika mala kan thermon pothe sugkatapsukhei d eauto to soma ten men gar epikteton ou phulattei thermasian oti phusei psukhron en to de med alloiousthai ten ousian autou pros emon alla mallon alloioun te kai metaballein emas out ekthermainetai pou pros emon auto te diatithesin emas kath eauto psukhron oun uparkhon phusei psukhei depou kai emas oukoun ouket aporon ouden upoloipon en to logo kai gar de kai oti touton apanton ton phusei psukhron o ti an epi pleon ekthermenes existatai tes idias phuseos pros to meden aporon ekhein eti kai marturei tois proeiremenois os gar kai e salamandra mekhri men tinos ouden upo puros paskhei katakaietai d ei pleiona khronon plesiaseien outo kai mandragoras kai koneion kai mekonion kai psullion epi brakhu men omilesanta puri ten oikeian eti diaphulattei krasin epi pleon de thermanthenta diaphtheiretai parakhrema kai dran ouket ouden on proteron epephukei dunatai ton men de toiouton apanton e phusis enantiotate tois anthropois esti phusin d otan eipo ten olen ousian te kai krasin lego ten ek ton proton stoikheion thermou kai psukhrou kai xerou kai ugrou ton de ge takhista trephonton oikeiotate ta d alla panta metaxu touton esti ta men mallon ta d etton dran kai paskhein upo tou somatos emon dunamena kastorion men kai peperi dran mallon e paskhein upo tou somatos emon dunamena oinos de kai meli kai ptisane paskhein mallon e dran apanta goun tauta kai paskhei ti kai dra peri to soma kath olou gar epeidan eis tauton allelois ekonta duo somata diamakhetai te kai stasiaze pros allela peri tes alloioseos en khrono pleioni dran kai paskhein ekateron auton anagkaion estin isos de kan me panu pollo khrono gignetai touto dra men ti kai tote to nikomenon eis to kratoun all outo smikron os lanthanein ten aisthesin oude gar o tmetikotatos sideros ei ton malakotaton temnoi keron di oles emeras kai nuktos dunaton auto me ouk amblei genesthai saphos outo depou kakeino kalos eiresthai dokei petren koilainei ranis udatos endelekheie kai gar kai phainetai gignomenon outos all epi mias e kai deuteras prosboles ouden oupo saphes en tois toioutois idein estin othen oimai kai to med olos paskhein enia pros ton omilounton edoxasthe tisi kai sugkhoreteon ge tois outo legousi pollakis kai autous omoios ekeinois lekteon esti ta polla plen ei pote mekhri tes eskhates akribeias anagoimen ton logon osper en to paronti poioumen outos oun kai to tes aeipatheias dogma
0 Herodotus1 epempon es delphous theopropous epeiresomenous to antixoon e de puthie sphi os autoi knidioi legousi khra en trimetro tono tade isthmon de me purgoute med orussete zeus gar k etheke neson ei k ebouleto knidioi men tauta tes puthies khresases tou te orugmatos epausanto kai arpago epionti sun to strato amakheti spheas autous paredosan esan de pedasees oikeontes uper alikarnessou mesogaian toisi okos ti melloi anepitedeon esesthai autoisi te kai toisi perioikoisi e ireie tes athenaies pogona megan iskhe tris sphi touto egeneto outoi ton peri karien andron mounoi te anteskhon khronon arpago kai pregmata pareskhon pleista oros teikhisantes to ounoma esti lide pedasees men nun khrono exairethesan lukioi de os es to ksanthion pedion elase o arpagos ton straton epexiontes kai makhomenoi oligoi pros pollous aretas apedeiknunto essothentes de kai kateilethentes es to astu sunelisan es ten akropolin tas te gunaikas kai ta tekna kai ta khremata kai tous oiketas kai epeita upepsan ten akropolin pasan tauten kaiesthai tauta de poiesantes kai sunomosantes orkous deinous epexelthontes apethanon pantes ksanthioi makhomenoi ton de nun lukion phamenon ksanthion einai oi polloi plen ogdokonta istieon eisi epeludes ai de ogdokonta istiai autai etukhon tenikauta ekdemeousi kai outo periegenonto ten men de ksanthon outo eskhe o arpagos paraplesios de kai ten kaunon eskhe kai gar oi kaunioi tous lukious emimesanto ta pleo ta men nun kato tes asies arpagos anastata epoiee ta de ano autes autos kuros pan ethnos katastrephomenos kai ouden parieis ta men nun auton pleo paresomen ta de oi pareskhe te ponon pleiston kai axiapegetotata esti touton epimnesomai kuros epeite ta panta tes epeirou upokheiria epoiesato assurioisi epetitheto tes de assuries esti men kou kai alla polismata megala polla to de onomastotaton kai iskhurotaton kai entha sphi ninou anastatou genomenes ta basileia katestekee en babulon eousa toiaute de tis polis keetai en pedio megalo megathos eousa metopon ekaston eikosi kai ekaton stadion eouses tetragonou outoi stadioi tes periodou tes polios ginontai sunapantes ogdokonta kai tetrakosioi to men nun megathos tosouton esti tou asteos tou babuloniou ekekosmeto de os ouden allo polisma ton emeis idmen taphros men prota min bathea te kai eurea kai plee udatos peritheei meta de teikhos pentekonta men pekheon basileion eon to euros upsos de diekosion pekheon o de basileios pekhus tou metriou esti pekheos mezon trisi daktuloisi dei de me pros toutoisi eti phrasai ina te ek tes taphrou e ge anaisimothe kai to teikhos ontina tropon ergasto orussontes ama ten taphron eplintheuon ten gen ten ek tou orugmatos ekpheromenen elkusantes de plinthous ikanas optesan autas en kaminoisi meta de telmati khreomenoi asphalto therme kai dia triekonta domon plinthou tarsous kalamon diastoibazontes edeiman prota men tes taphou ta kheilea deutera de auto to teikhos ton auton tropon epano de tou teikheos para ta eskhata oikemata mounokola edeiman tetrammena es allela to meson de ton oikematon elipon tethrippo perielasin pulai de enestasi perix tou teikheos ekaton khalkeai pasai kai stathmoi te kai uperthura osautos esti de alle polis apekhousa okto emereon odon apo babulonos is ounoma aute entha esti potamos ou megas is kai to potamo to ounoma esballei de outos es ton euphreten potamon to reethron outos on o is potamos ama to udati thrombous asphaltou anadidoi pollous enthen e asphaltos es to en babuloni teikhos ekomisthe eteteikhisto men nun e babulon tropo toiode esti de duo pharsea tes polios to gar meson autes potamos diergei to ounoma esti euphretes reei de ex armenion eon megas kai bathus kai takhus exiei de outos es ten eruthren thalassan to on de teikhos ekateron tous agkonas es ton potamon elelatai to de apo toutou ai epikampai para kheilos ekateron tou potamou aimasie plinthon opteon parateinei to de astu auto eon pleres oikieon triorophon kai tetrorophon katatetmetai tas odous itheas tas te allas kai tas epikarsias tas epi ton potamon ekhousas kata de on ekasten odon en te aimasie te para ton potamon pulides epesan osai per ai laurai tosautai arithmon esan de kai autai khalkeai pherousai kai autai es auton ton potamon touto men de to teikhos thorex esti eteron de esothen teikhos peritheei ou pollo teo asthenesteron tou eterou teikheos steinoteron de en de pharsei ekatero tes polios eteteikhisto en meso en to men ta basileia peribolo megalo te kai iskhuro en de to etero dios belou iron khalkopulon kai es eme eti touto eon duo stadion pante eon tetragonon en meso de tou irou purgos stereos oikodometai stadiou kai to mekos kai to euros kai epi touto to purgo allos purgos epibebeke kai eteros mala epi touto mekhri ou okto purgon anabasis de es autous exothen kuklo peri pantas tous purgous ekhousa pepoietai mesounti de kou tes anabasios esti katagoge te kai thokoi ampausterioi en toisi katizontes ampauontai oi anabainontes en de to teleutaio purgo neos epesti megas en de to neo kline megale keetai eu estromene kai oi trapeza parakeetai khrusee agalma de ouk eni ouden autothi enidrumenon oude nukta oudeis enaulizetai anthropon oti me gune moune ton epikhorion ten an o theos eletai ek paseon os legousi oi khaldaioi eontes irees toutou tou theou phasi de oi autoi outoi emoi men ou pista legontes ton theon auton phoitan te es ton neon kai ampauesthai epi tes klines kata per en thebesi tesi aiguptiesi kata ton auton tropon os legousi oi aiguptioi kai gar de ekeithi koimatai en to tou dios tou thebaieos gune amphoterai de autai legontai andron oudamon es omilien phoitan kai kata per en pataroisi tes lukies e promantis tou theou epean genetai ou gar on aiei esti khresterion autothi epean de genetai tote on sugkatakleietai tas nuktas eso en to neo esti de tou en babuloni irou kai allos kato neos entha agalma mega tou dios eni katemenon khruseon kai oi trapeza megale parakeetai khrusee kai to bathron oi kai o thronos khruseos esti kai os elegon oi khaldaioi talanton oktakosion khrusiou pepoietai tauta exo de tou neou bomos esti khruseos esti de kai allos bomos megas ep ou thuetai ta telea ton probaton epi gar tou khruseou bomou ouk exesti thuein oti me galathena mouna epi de tou mezonos bomou kai katagizousi libanotou khilia talanta eteos ekastou oi khaldaioi tote epean ten orten agosi to theo touto en de en to temenei touto eti ton khronon ekeinon kai andrias duodeka pekheon khruseos stereos ego men min ouk eidon ta de legetai upo khaldaion tauta lego touto to andrianti dareios men o ustaspeos epibouleusas ouk etolmese labein kserxes de o dareiou elabe kai ton irea apekteine apagoreuonta me kineein ton andrianta to men de iron touto outo kekosmetai esti de kai idia anathemata polla tes de babulonos tautes polloi men kou kai alloi egenonto basilees ton en toisi assurioisi logoisi mnemen poiesomai oi ta teikhea te epekosmesan kai ta ira en de de kai gunaikes duo e men proteron arxasa tes usteron geneesi pente proteron genomene te ounoma en semiramis aute men apedexato khomata ana to pedion eonta axiotheeta proteron de eothee o potamos ana to pedion pan pelagizein e de de deuteron genomene tautes basileia te ounoma en nitokris aute de sunetotere genomene tes proteron arxases touto men mnemosuna elipeto ta ego apegesomai touto de ten medon orosa arkhen megalen te kai ouk atremizousan all alla te arairemena astea autoisi en de de kai amphotera tauta ton te potamon skolion kai to orugma pan elos os o te potamos braduteros eie peri kampas pollas agnumenos kai oi plooi eosi skolioi es ten babulona ek te ton ploon ekdeketai periodos tes limnes makre kata touto de ergazeto tes khores te ai te esbolai esan kai ta suntoma tes ek medon odou ina me epimisgomenoi oi medoi ekmanthanoien autes ta pregmata tauta men de ek batheos diabenai khren ploio diabainein kai en os ego dokeo okhleron touto aute de kai touto proeide epeite gar orusse to elutron te limne mnemosunon tode allo apo tou autou ergou elipeto etamneto lithous perimekeas os de oi esan oi lithoi etoimoi kai to khorion ororukto ektrepsasa tou potamou to reethron pan es to orusse khorion en o epimplato touto en touto apexerasmenou tou arkhaiou reethrou touto men ta kheilea tou potamou kata ten polin kai tas katabasias tas ek ton pulidon es ton potamon pherousas anoikodomese plinthoisi optesi kata ton auton logon to teikhei touto de kata mesen kou malista ten polin toisi lithoisi tous oruxato oikodomee gephuran deousa tous lithous sidero te kai molubdo epiteineske de ep auten okos men emere ginoito xula tetragona ep on ten diabasin epoieunto oi babulonioi tas de nuktas ta xula tauta apaireeskon toude eineka ina me diaphoiteontes tas nuktas kleptoien par allelon os de to te orukhthen limne pleres egegonee upo tou potamou kai ta peri ten gephuran ekekosmeto ton euphreten potamon es ta arkhaia reethra ek tes limnes exegage kai outo to orukhthen elos genomenon es deon edokee gegonenai kai toisi polietesi gephura en kateskeuasmene e d aute aute basileia kai apaten toiende tina emekhanesato uper ton malista leophoron puleon tou asteos taphon eoute kateskeuasato meteoron epipoles auteon ton puleon enekolapse de es ton taphon grammata tou patros tou eoutou tounoma labunetou kai ten assurion arkhen strateuetai de de basileus o megas kai sitioisi eu eskeuasmenos ex oikou kai probatoisi kai de kai udor apo tou khoaspeo potamou ama oste tou loipou kai gunaikas min eupeteos to gonu ou brekhousas diabesesthai meta de ten apeilen meteis ten epi babulona strateusin diairee ten stratien dikha dielon de kateteine skhoinoteneas upodexas diorukhas ogdokonta kai ekaton par ekateron to kheilos tou gundeo tetrammenas panta tropon diataxas de ton straton orussein ekeleue oia de omilou pollou ergazomenou eneto men to ergon omos ten babulona oi de babulonioi ekstrateusamenoi emenon auton epei de egeneto elaunon agkhou tes polios sunebalon te oi babulonioi kai essothentes te makhe kateilethesan es to astu oia de exepistamenoi ton potamon kai kata ten limnen epoiee kai o kuros etera toiauta ton gar potamon diorukhi esagagon es ten limnen eousan elos to arkhaion reethron diabaton einai epoiese uponostesantos tou potamou genomenou de toutou toioutou oi persai oi per etetakhato ep auto touto kata to reethron tou euphreteo potamou uponenostekotos andri os es meson meron malista ke kata touto eseisan es ten babulona ei men nun proeputhonto e emathon oi babulonioi to ek tou kurou poieumenon oi d an periidontes tous persas eselthein es ten polin diephtheiran an kakista katakleisantes gar an pasas tas es ton potamon pulidas ekhousas kai autoi epi tas aimasias anabantes tas para ta kheilea tou potamou elelamenas elabon an spheas os en kurte nun de ex aprosdoketou sphi parestesan oi persai upo de megatheos tes polios os legetai upo ton taute oikemenon ton peri ta eskhata tes polios ealokoton tous to meson oikeontas ton babulonion ou manthanein ealokotas alla tukhein gar sphi eousan orten khoreuein te touton tode basilei to megalo es trophen autou te kai tes straties diarairetai parex tou phorou ge pasa oses arkhei duodeka on menon eonton es ton eniauton tous tesseras menas trephei min e babulonie khore kratiste okou tritantaikhme to artabazou ek basileos ekhonti ton nomon touton arguriou men proseie ekastes emeres artabe meste e de artabe metron eon persikon khoreei medimnou attikou pleon khoinixi trisi attikesi ippoi de oi autou esan idie parex ton polemisterion oi men anabainontes tas theleas oktakosioi ai de bainomenai exakiskhiliai kai muriai anebaine gar ekastos ton ersenon touton eikosi babulonos uperkhe eonta e de ge ton assurion uetai men oligo kai to ektrephon ten rizan tou sitou esti touto ardomenon mentoi ek tou potamou adrunetai te to leion kai paraginetai o sitos ou kata per 0 HippocratesAncientMedicine mekhri de toutou pollou moi dokei dein lego de tauten ten istorien eidenai anthropos ti estin kai di oias aitias ginetai kai talla akribeos epei touto ge moi dokei anagkaion einai ietro peri phusios eidenai kai panu spoudasai os eisetai eiper ti mellei ton deonton poiesein o ti te estin anthropos pros ta esthiomena te kai pinomena kai o ti pros ta alla epitedeumata kai o ti aph ekastou ekasto sumbesetai kai me aplos outos poneron estin broma turos ponon gar parekhei to plerothenti autou alla tina te ponon kai dia ti kai tini ton en to anthropo eneonton anepitedeion esti gar kai alla polla bromata kai pomata ponera a diatithesi ton anthropon ou ton auton tropon outos oun moi esto oion oinos akretos pollos potheis diatithesi pos ton anthropon kai pantes an oi eidotes touto gnoiesan oti aute dunamis oinou kai autos aitios kai oisi ge ton en to anthropo touto dunatai malista oidamen toiauten de boulomai aletheien kai peri ton allon phanenai turos gar epeide touto semeio ekhresamen ou pantas anthropous omoios lumainetai all eisin oitines autou pleroumenoi oud otioun blaptontai alla kai iskhun oisin an sumphere thaumasios parekhetai eisi d oi khalepos apallassousi diapherousin oun touton ai phusies diapherousin de kata touto oper en to somati enesti polemion turo kai upo toutou egeiretai te kai kineitai ois o toioutos khumos tugkhanei pleion eneon kai mallon endunasteuon en to somati toutous mallon kai kakopathein eikos ei de pase te anthropine phusei en kakon pantas an elumenato tauta de ei tis eideie ouk an paskhoi tade en tesin anakomidesi tesin ek ton nouson eti de kai en tesi nousoisi tesi makresi ginontai pollai suntaraxies ai men apo toutomatou ai de kai apo ton prosenekhthenton ton tukhonton oida de tous pollous ietrous osper tous idiotas en tukhosi peri ten emeren tauten ti kekainourgekotes e lousamenoi e peripatesantes e phagontes ti eteroion tauta de panta beltio prosenenegmena e me ouden esson ten aitien touton tini anatithentas kai to men aition agnoeuntas to de sumphorotaton en outo tukhe aphaireontas dei de ou all eidenai ti loutron akairos prosgenomenon ergasetai e ti kopos oudepote gar e aute kakopatheia touton oudeterou oude ge apo plerosios oud apo bromatos toiou e toiou ostis oun tauta me eisetai os ekasta ekhei pros ton anthropon oute ginoskein ta ginomena ap auton dunesetai oute khresthai orthos dein de moi dokei kai tauta eidenai osa to anthropo pathemata apo dunamion ginetai kai osa apo skhematon lego de ti toiouton dunamin men einai ton khumon tas akrotetas te kai iskhun skhemata de lego osa enestin en to anthropo ta men koila te kai ex eureos es stenon sunegmena ta de kai ekpeptamena ta de sterea te kai stroggula ta de platea te kai epikremamena ta de diatetamena ta de makra ta de pukna ta de mana te kai tethelota ta de spoggoeidea te kai araia touto men oun elkusai eph eouto kai epispasasthai ugroteta ek tou allou somatos poteron ta koila te kai ekpeptamena e ta sterea te kai stroggula e ta koila te kai es stenon ex eureos sunegmena dunaito an malista oimai men ta toiauta ta es stenon sunegmena ek koilou te kai eureos katamanthanein de dei tauta exothen ek ton phaneron touto men gar to stomati kekhenos ugron ouden anaspaseis promullenas de kai susteilas piesas te ta kheilea kai epeiten
0 HomerOdyssey1-12 kheontas os d ot an agrauloi pories peri bous agelaias elthousas es kopron epen botanes koresontai pasai ama skairousin enantiai oud eti sekoi iskhous all adinon mukomenai amphitheousi meteras os em ekeinoi epei idon ophthalmoisi dakruoentes ekhunto dokese d ara sphisi thumos os emen os ei patrid ikoiato kai polin auten trekheies ithakes ina t etraphen ed egenonto kai m olophuromenoi epea pteroenta proseudon soi men nostesanti diotrephes os ekharemen os ei t eis ithaken aphikoimetha patrida gaian all age ton allon etaron katalexon olethron os ephan autar ego prosephen malakois epeessi nea men ar pamproton erussomen epeironde ktemata d en speessi pelassomen opla te panta autoi d otrunesthe emoi ama pantes epesthai ophra ideth etarous ierois en domasi kirkes pinontas kai edontas epeetanon gar ekhousin os ephamen oi d oka emois epeessi pithonto eurulokhos de moi oios erukane pantas etairous kai spheas phonesas epea pteroenta proseuda a deiloi pos imen ti kakon imeirete touton kirkes es megaron katabemenai e ken apantas e sus ee lukous poiesetai ee leontas oi ken oi mega doma phulassoimen kai anagke os per kuklops erx ote oi messaulon ikonto emeteroi etaroi sun d o thrasus eipet odusseus toutou gar kai keinoi atasthaliesin olonto os ephat autar ego ge meta phresi mermerixa spassamenos tanuekes aor pakheos para merou to oi apoplexas periphron alla pithesthe alkinoou d ek toud ekhetai ergon te epos te ton d aut alkinoos apameibeto phonesen te touto men outo de estai epos ai ken ego ge zoos phaiekessi phileretmoisin anasso xeinos de tleto mala per nostoio khatizon empes oun epimeinai es aurion eis o ke pasan dotinen teleso pompe d andressi melesei pasi malista d emoi tou gar kratos est eni demo ton d apameibomenos prosephe polumetis odusseus alkinoe kreion panton arideikete laon ei me kai eis eniauton anogoit autothi mimnein pompen d otrunoite kai aglaa dora didoite kai ke to bouloimen kai ken polu kerdion eie pleiotere sun kheiri philen es patrid ikesthai kai k aidoioteros kai philteros andrasin eien pasin osoi m ithakende idoiato nostesanta ton d aut alkinoos apameibeto phonesen te o oduseu to men ou ti s eiskomen eisoroontes eperopea t emen kai epiklopon oia te pollous boskei gaia melaina poluspereas anthropous pseudea t artunontas othen ke tis oude idoito soi d epi men morphe epeon eni de phrenes esthlai muthon d os ot aoidos epistamenos katelexas panton t argeion seo t autou kedea lugra all age moi tode eipe kai atrekeos katalexon ei tinas antitheon etaron ides oi toi am auto ilion eis am eponto kai autou potmon epespon nux d ede mala makre athesphatos oude po ore eudein en megaro su de moi lege theskela erga kai ken es eo dian anaskhoimen ote moi su tlaies en megaro ta sa kedea muthesasthai ton d apameibomenos prosephe polumetis odusseus alkinoe kreion panton arideikete laon ore men poleon muthon ore de kai upnou ei d et akouemenai ge lilaieai ouk an ego ge touton soi phthoneoimi kai oiktroter all agoreuein kede emon etaron oi de metopisthen olonto oi troon men upexephugon stonoessan auten en nosto d apolonto kakes ioteti gunaikos autar epei psukhas men apeskedas alludis alle agne persephoneia gunaikon theluteraon elthe d epi psukhe agamemnonos atreidao akhnumene peri d allai agegerath ossoi am auto oiko en aigisthoio thanon kai potmon epespon egno d aips em ekeinos epei pien aima kelainon klaie d o ge ligeos thaleron kata dakruon eibon pitnas eis eme kheiras orexasthai meneainon all ou gar oi et en is empedos oude ti kikus oie per paros esken eni gnamptoisi melessi ton men ego dakrusa idon eleesa te thumo kai min phonesas epea pteroenta proseudon atreide kudiste anax andron agamemnon tis nu se ker edamasse tanelegeos thanatoio ee se g en neessi poseidaon edamassen orsas argaleon anemon amegarton autmen ee s anarsioi andres edelesant epi khersou bous peritamnomenon ed oion poea kala ee peri ptolios makheoumenon ede gunaikon os ephamen o de m autik ameibomenos proseeipe diogenes laertiade polumekhan odusseu out eme g en neessi poseidaon edamassen orsas argaleon anemon amegarton autmen oute m anarsioi andres edelesant epi khersou alla moi aigisthos teuxas thanaton te moron te ekta sun oulomene alokho oikonde kalessas deipnissas os tis te katektane boun epi phatne os thanon oiktisto thanato peri d alloi etairoi nolemeos kteinonto sues os argiodontes oi ra t en aphneiou andros mega dunamenoio e gamo e erano e eilapine tethaluie ede men poleon phono andron antebolesas mounax kteinomenon kai eni kratere usmine alla ke keina malista idon olophurao thumo os amphi kretera trapezas te plethousas keimeth eni megaro dapedon d apan aimati thuen oiktrotaten d ekousa opa priamoio thugatros kassandres ten kteine klutaimnestre dolometis amph emoi autar ego poti gaie kheiras aeiron ballon apothneskon peri phasgano e de kunopis nosphisat oude moi etle ionti per eis aidao khersi kat ophthalmous eleein sun te stom ereisai os ouk ainoteron kai kunteron allo gunaikos e tis de toiauta meta phresin erga baletai oion de kai keine emesato ergon aeikes kouridio teuxasa posei phonon e toi ephen ge aspasios paidessin ide dmoessin emoisin oikad eleusesthai e d exokha lugra iduia oi te kat aiskhos ekheue kai essomenesin opisso theluteresi gunaixi kai e k euergos eesin os ephat autar ego min ameibomenos proseeipon o popoi e mala de gonon atreos euruopa zeus ekpaglos ekhthere gunaikeias dia boulas ex arkhes elenes men apolometh eineka polloi soi de klutaimnestre dolon ertue teloth eonti os ephamen o de m autik ameibomenos proseeipe to nun me pote kai su gunaiki per epios einai me oi muthon apanta piphauskemen on k eu eides alla to men phasthai to de kai kekrummenon einai all ou soi g oduseu phonos essetai ek ge gunaikos lien gar pinute te kai eu phresi medea oide koure ikarioio periphron penelopeia e men min numphen ge neen kateleipomen emeis erkhomenoi polemonde pais de oi en epi mazo nepios os pou nun ge met andron izei arithmo olbios e gar ton ge pater philos opsetai elthon kai keinos patera prosptuxetai e themis estin e d eme oude per uios eniplesthenai akoitis ophthalmoisin ease paros de me pephne kai auton allo de toi ereo su d eni phresi balleo sesin krubden med anaphanda philen es patrida gaian nea katiskhemenai epei ouketi pista gunaixin all age moi tode eipe kai atrekeos katalexon ei pou eti zoontos akouete paidos emoio e pou en orkhomeno e en pulo emathoenti e pou par menelao eni sparte eureie ou gar po tethneken epi khthoni dios orestes os ephat autar ego min ameibomenos proseeipon atreide ti me tauta dieireai oude ti oida zoei o g e tethneke kakon d anemolia bazein noi men os epeessin ameibomeno stugeroisin estamen akhnumenoi
0 JustinMartyrApology1 oun kai skhematos tou phainomenou ose dunamis protrepsamenoi umas aneuthunoi oidamen loipon ontes kan umeis apistete to gar emeteron gegone kai peperantai ouk erkesthesan de oi phauloi daimones pro tes phaneroseos tou khristou eipein tous lekhthentas uious to dii gegonenai all epeide phanerothentos autou kai genomenou en anthropois kai opos dia ton propheton proekekerukto emathon kai en panti genei pisteuomenon kai prosdokomenon egnosan palin os proedelosamen proeballonto allous simona men kai menandron apo samareias oi kai magikas dunameis poiesantes pollous exepatesan kai eti apatomenous ekhousi kai gar par umin os proephemen en te basilidi rome epi klaudiou kaisaros genomenos o simon kai ten ieran sugkleton kai ton demon romaion eis tosouto kateplexato os theon nomisthenai kai andrianti os tous allous par umin timomenous theous timethenai othen ten te ieran sugkleton kai ton demon ton umeteron sunepignomonas tautes emon tes axioseos paralabein aitoumen in ei tis eie tois ap ekeinou didagmasi katekhomenos talethes mathon ten planen phugein dunethe kai ton andrianta ei boulesthe kathairesate ou gar me genesthai ten ekpurosin epi kolasei ton asebon oi phauloi daimones peisai dunantai onper tropon oude lathein ton khriston paragenomenon iskhusan praxai all ekeino monon tous alogos biountas kai empathos en ethesi phaulois tethrammenous kai philodoxountas anairein emas kai misein dunantai poiesai ous ou monon ou misoumen all os deiknutai eleountes metathesthai peisai boulometha ou gar dedoikamen thanaton tou pantos apothanein omologoumenou kai medenos allou kainoi all e ton aiton en tede te dioikesei onton on ei me koros tous metaskhontas kan eniautou ekhe ina aei osi kai apatheis kai anendeeis tois emeterois didagmasi prosekhein dei ei d apistousi meden einai meta thanaton all eis anaisthesian khorein tous apothneskontas apophainontai pathon ton entautha kai khreion emas ruomenoi euergetousin eautous de phaulous kai misanthropous kai philodoxous deiknuousin ou gar os apallaxontes emas anairousin all os posterountes zoes kai edones phoneuousi kai markiona de ton apo pontou a s proephemen proeballonto oi phauloi daimones os arneisthai men ton poieten ton ouranion kai apanton theon kai ton prokerukhthenta dia ton propheton khriston uion autou kai nun didaskei allon de tina kataggellei para ton demiourgon ton panton theon kai omoios eteron uion o polloi peisthentes o s mono talethe epistameno emon katagelosin apodeixin medemian peri on legousin ekhontes alla alogos os upo lukou arnes sunerpasmenoi bora ton atheon dogmaton kai daimonon ginontai ou gar allo ti agonizontai oi legomenoi daimones e apagein tous anthropous apo tou poiesantos theou kai tou protogonou autou khristou kai tous men tes ges me epairesthai dunamenous tois kai kheiropoietois proselosan kai proselousi tous de epi theorian theion ormontas upekkrouontes en me logismon sophrona kai katharon kai apathe bion ekhosin eis asebeian emballousin ina de kai para ton emeteron didaskalon legomen de tou logou tou dia ton propheton labonta ton platona mathete to eipein ulen amorphon ousan strepsanta ton theon kosmon poiesai akousate ton autolexei eiremenon dia mouseos tou prodedelomenou protou prophetou kai presbuterou ton en ellesi suggrapheon di ou menuon to prophetikon pneuma pos ten arkhen kai ek tinon edemiourgesen o theos ton kosmon ephe outos en arkhe epoiesen o theos ton ouranon kai ten gen e de ge en aoratos kai akataskeuastos kai skotos epano tes abussou kai pneuma theou epephereto epano ton udaton kai eipen o theos genetheto phos kai egeneto outos oste logo theou ek ton upokeimenon kai prodelothenton dia mouseos gegenesthai ton panta kosmon kai platon kai oi tauta legontes kai emeis emathomen kai umeis peisthenai dunasthe kai to kaloumenon erebos para tois poietais eiresthai proteron upo mouseos oidamen kai to en to para platoni timaio phusiologoumenon peri tou uiou tou theou ote legei ekhiasen auton en ta panti para mouseos labon omoios eipen en gar tais mouseos graphais anagegraptai os kat ekeino tou kairou ote exelthon apo aiguptou oi israelitai kai gegonasin en te eremo apentesan autois iobola theria ekhidnai te kai aspides kai opheon pan genos o ethanatou ton laon kai kat epipnoian kai energeian ten para tou theou genomenen labein ton mousea khalkon kai poiesai tupon staurou kai touton stesai epi te agia skene kai eipein ta lao kan prosblepete to tupo touto kai pisteuete en auta sothesesthe kai genomenou toutou tous men opheis apothanein anegrapse ton de laon ekphugein ton thanaton outos paredoken a anagnous platon kai me akribos epistamenos mede noesas tupon einai staurou alla khiasma noesas ten meta ton proton theon dunamin kekhiasthai en to panti eipe kai ti eipein auton triton epeide os proeipomen epano ton udaton anegno upo mouseos eiremenon epipheresthai to tou theou pneuma deuteran men gar khoran ta para theou logo on kekhiasthai en ta panti ephe didosi ten de triten to lekhthenti epipheresthai to udati pneumati eipon ta de trita peri ton triton kai os ekpurosin genesesthai dia mouseos proemenuse to prophetikon pneuma akousate ephe de outos katabesetai aeizoon pur kai kataphagetai mekhri tes abussou kato ou ta auta oun emeis allois doxazomen all oi pantes ta emetera mimoumenoi legousi par emin oun esti tauta akousai kai mathein para ton oude tous kharakteras ton stoikheion epistamenon idioton men kai barbaron to phthegma sophon de kai piston ton noun onton kai peran kai kheron tinon tas opseis os suneinai ou sophia anthropeia tauta gegonenai alla dunamei theou legesthai on tropon de kai anethekamen eautous to theo kainopoiethentes dia tou khristou exegesometha opos me touto paralipontes doxomen ponereuein ti en te exegesei osoi an peisthosi kai pisteuosin alethe tauta ta uph emon didaskomena kai legomena einai kai bioun outos dunasthai upiskhnontai eukhesthai te kai aitein nesteuontes para tou theou ton proemartemenon aphesin didaskontai emon suneukhomenon kai sunnesteuonton autois epeita agontai uph emon entha udor esti kai tropon anagenneseos on kai emeis autoi anegennethemen anagennontai ep onomatos gar tou patros ton olon kai despotou theou kai tou soteros emon iesou khristou kai pneumatos agiou to en to udati tote loutron poiountai kai gar o khristos eipen an me anagennethete ou me eiselthete eis ten basileian ton ouranon oti de kai adunaton eis tas metras ton tekouson tous apax gennomenous embenai phaneron pasin esti kai dia esaiou tou prophetou os proegrapsamen eiretai tina tropon pheuxontai tas amartias oi amartesantes kai metanoountes elekhthe de outos lousasthe katharoi genesthe aphelete tas ponerias apo ton psukhon umon mathete kalon poiein krinate orphano kai dikaiosate kheran kai deute kai dialekhthomen legei kurios kai ean osin ai amartiai umon os phoinikoun osei erion leukano kai ean osin os kokkinon os khiona leukano ean de me eisakousete mou makhaira umas katedetai to gar stoma kuriou elalese tauta kai logon de eis touto para ton apostolon emathomen touton epeide ten proten genesin emon agnoountes kat anagken gegennemetha ex ugras sporas kata mixin ten ton goneon pros allelous kai en ethesi phaulois kai ponerais anastrophais gegonamen opos me anagkes tekna mede agnoias menomen alla proaireseos kai epistemes apheseos amartion on proemartomen tukhomen en to udati eponomazetai to elomeno anagennethenai kai metanoesanti epi tois emartemenois to tou patros ton olon kai despotou theou onoma auto touto monon epilegontos tou ton lousomenon agontos epi to loutron onoma gar to theo oudeis ekhei eipein ei de tis tolmeseien einai legein memene ten asoton manian kaleitai de touto to loutron photismos os photizomenon ten dianoian ton tauta manthanonton kai ep onomatos de iesou khristou tou staurothentos epi pontiou pilatou kai ep onomatos pneumatos agiou o dia ton propheton proekeruxe ta kata ton iesoun panta o photizomenos louetai kai to loutron de touto akousantes oi daimones dia tou prophetou kekerugmenon energesan kai rantizein eautous tous eis ta iera auton epibainontas kai prosienai autois mellontas loibas kai knisas apotelountas teleon de kai louesthai epiontas prin elthein epi ta iera entha idruntai energousi kai gar to upoluesthai epibainontas tois ierois kai tois autois tous threskeuontas keleuesthai upo ton ierateuonton ek ton sumbanton mousei to eiremeno prophete mathontes oi daimones emimesanto kat ekeino gar tou kairou ote mouses ekeleusthe katelthon eis aigupton exagagein ton ekei laon ton israeliton poimainontos autou en te ge probata tou pros metros theiou en idea puros ek batou prosomilesen auto o emeteros khristos kai eipen upolusai ta upodemata sou kai proselthon akouson o de upolusamenos kai proselthon akekoe katelthein eis aigupton kai exagagein ton ekei laon ton israeliton kai dunamin iskhuran elabe para tou lalesantos auto en idea puros khristou kai katelthon exegage ton laon poiesas megala kai thaumasia a ei boulesthe mathein ek ton suggrammaton ekeinou akribos mathesesthe ioudaioi de pantes kai nun didaskousi ton anonomaston theon lelalekenai to mousei othen to prophetikon pneuma dia esaiou tou promemenumenou prophetou elegkhon autous os proegrapsamen eipen egno bous ton ktesamenon kai onos ten phatnen tou kuriou autou israel de me ouk egno kai o laos me ou suneke kai iesous de o khristos oti ouk egnosan ioudaioi ti pater kai ti uios omoios elegkhon autous kai autos eipen
0 LucianTyrannicide lupen ten apognosin ton phobon tas epi ton mellonton tas epi ton mellonton ton epi ton mellonton tas epi ton mellonton elpidas khronon elpidas poneras toutois oun ep auton ekhresamen tois summakhois kai pros pros roiou peri epi ten teleutaian ekeinen skepsin katenagkasa apethanen umin ateknos lelupemenos oduromenos dakruon pepenthekos penthos oligokhronion men all ikanon patri kai to deinotaton autos uph autou osper thanaton oiktistos kai pollo khalepoteros e ei up allou gignoito pou moi to xiphos me tis allos touto tou gnorizei me tinos allou oplon touto tou en tis auto es ten akropolin anekomise pro tou turannou tis tis n ekhresato tis auto ep ekeinon apesteilen o xiphos koinonon kai diadokhon ton emon katorthomaton meta tosoutous kindunous meta tosoutous phonous ameloumetha kai anaxioi dokoumen doreas ei gar uper monou toutou ten timen etoun par umon ei gar elegon andres apothanein ethelesanti to turanno kai anoplo epi tou kairou kateilemmeno xiphos touto tou emon uperetese kai pros to telos tes eleutherias sunergese pante panti pante touto tou times te kai doreas axion nomisate despoten outo demotikou ktematos ouk an emeipsasthe ouk an en tois euergetais anegrapsate ouk an to xiphos en tois ierois anethekate ouk an meta ton theon kakeino prosekunesate nun moi ennoesate oia pepoiekenai eikos ton turannon oia de eirekenai pro tes teleutes epei gar up emou phoneuomenos kai titroskomenos pollois traumasin es ta phanera tou somatos os an malista lupesein emellon ton gegennekota os an ek tes protes theas diasparaxein o men aneboesen oiktron epiboomenos ton gegennekota ou boethon oude summakhon edei gar presbuten onta kai asthene alla theaten ton oikeion kakon ego gar gar apellattomen poietes men tes oles tragodias gegenemenos katalipon de to upokrite ton nekron kai ten skenen kai to xiphos kai ta loipa tou dramatos epistas de ekeinos kai idon uion
0 LysiasonEratosthenes gar o andres oper kai proteron eipon philos on sostratos kai oikeios diakeimenos apantesas ex agrou peri eliou dusmas sunedeipnei kai epeide kalos eikhen auto apion okheto kaitoi proton men o andres enthumethete oti oti ei en ekeine te nukti ego epebouleuon eratosthenei poteron en moi kreitton auto eterothi deipnein e ton sundeipnesonta moi eisagagein outo gar an etton etolmesen ekeinos eiselthein eis ten oikian eita doko an umin ton sundeipnounta apheis monos kataleiphthenai kai eremos genesthai e keleuein ekeinon meinai meinai men einai menein ina met emou ton moikhon etimoreito epeita o andres ouk an doko umin tois epitedeiois meth emeran paraggeilai kai keleusai autous sullegenai eis oikian tou tou ton philon eggutato mallon e epeide takhista esthomen tes nuktos peritrekhein ouk eidos ontina oikoi katalepsomai kai ontina exo kai os armodion men kai ton deina elthon ouk epidemountas ou gar ede eterous de ouk endon ontas katelabon ous d oios te e labon ebadizon kaitoige ei proede ouk an doko umin kai therapontas paraskeuasasthai kai tois philois paraggeilai in os asphalestata men autos eisea ti gar ede ei ti kakeinos eikhe siderion os meta pleiston de marturon ten timorian epoioumen nun d ouden eidos ton esomenon ekeine te nukti ous oios te e parelabon kai moi anabete touton martures martures ton men marturon akekoate o andres skepsasthe de par umin autois outos peri toutou tou pragmatos zetountes ei tis emoi kai eratosthenei ekhthra popote gegenetai plen tautes oudemian gar euresete oute gar
0 MarcusAurelius phusei o pepaideumenos kai aidemon legei dos o theleis apolabe o theleis legei de touto ou katathrasunomenos alla peitharkhon monon kai eunoon aute oligon esti to upoleipomenon touto zeson os en orei ouden gar diapherei ekei e ode ean tis pantakhou os en polei to kosmo idetosan istoresatosan oi anthropoi anthropon alethinon kata phusin zonta ei me pherousin apokteinatosan kreitton gar e outos zen meketh olos peri tou oion tina einai ton agathon andra dialegesthai alla einai toiouton tou olou aionos kai tes oles ousias sunekhos phantasia kai oti panta ta kata meros os men pros ousian kegkhramis os de pros khronon trupanou peristrophe eis ekaston ton upokeimenon ephistanta epinoein auto ede dialuomenon kai en metabole kai oion sepsei e skedasei ginomenon e kathoti ekaston pephuken osper thneskein oioi eisin esthiontes katheudontes okheuontes apopatountes ta alla eita oioi andronomoumenoi kai gauroumenoi e khalepainontes kai ex uperokhes epiplettontes pro oligou de edouleuon posois kai di oia kai met oligon en toioutois esontai sumpherei ekasto o pherei ekasto e ton olon phusis kai tote sumpherei ote ekeine pherei era men ombrou gaia era de o semnos aither era de o kosmos poiesai o an melle ginesthai lego oun to kosmo oti soi sunero meti de outo kakeino legetai oti philei touto ginesthai etoi entautha zes kai ede eithikas e exo upageis kai touto etheles e apothneskeis kai apeleitourgesas para de tauta ouden oukoun euthumei enarges esto aei to oti toiouto ekeino o agros esti kai pos panta esti ta auta enthade tois en akro to orei e epi tou aigialou e opou theleis antikrus gar eureseis ta tou platonos sekon en orei phesi periballomenos kai bdallon blekhemata ti esti moi to egemonikon mou kai poion ti auto ego poio nun kai pros ti pote auto nun khromai meti kenon nou esti meti apoluton kai apespasmenon koinonias meti prostetekos kai anakekramenon to sarkidio oste touto suntrepesthai o ton kurion pheugon drapetes kurios de o nomos kai o paranomon oun drapetes alla kai o lupoumenos e orgizomenos e phoboumenos ou bouletai ti gegonenai e ginesthai e genesesthai ton upo tou ta panta dioikountos tetagmenon os esti nomos nemon osa ekasto epiballei o ara phoboumenos e lupoumenos e orgizomenos drapetes sperma eis metran apheis apekhorese kai loipon alle aitia paralabousa ergazetai kai apotelei brephos ex oiou oion palin trophen dia pharuggos apheke kai loipon alle aitia paralabousa aisthesin kai ormen kai to olon zoen kai romen kai alla osa kai oia poiei tauta oun en toiaute egkalupsei ginomena theorein kai ten dunamin outos oran os kai ten brithousan kai ten anophere oromen oukhi tois ophthalmois all oukh etton enargos sunekhos epinoein pos panta toiauta opoia nun ginetai kai prosthen egineto kai epinoein genesomena kai ola dramata kai skenas omoeideis osa ek peiras tes ses e tes presbuteras istorias egnos pro ommaton tithesthai oion aulen olen adrianou kai aulen olen antoninou kai aulen olen philippou alexandrou kroisou panta gar ekeina toiauta en monon di eteron phantazou panta ton eph otinioun lupoumenon e dusarestounta omoion to thuomeno khoiridio kai apolaktizonti kai kekragoti omoios kai o oimozon epi tou klinidiou monos siope ten endesin emon kai oti mono to logiko zoo dedotai to ekousios epesthai tois ginomenois to de epesthai psilon pasin anagkaion kata meros eph ekastou on poieis ephistanon eperota seauton ei o thanatos deinon dia to toutou steresthai otan proskoptes epi tinos amartia euthus metabas epilogizou ti paromoion amartaneis oion argurion agathon einai krinon e ten edonen e to doxarion kai kat eidos touto gar epiballon takheos epilese tes orges sumprospiptontos tou oti biazetai ti gar poiesei e ei dunasai aphele autou to biazomenon saturiona idon sokratikon phantazou e 0 OrigenAgainstCelsus1 ego d eipoim an oti peri men ton kometon oudemia propheteia pheretai os oti kata tende ten basileian e tousde tous khronous anatelei toiosde kometes peri de tou epi te genesei 0 Plotinus1 esti to aistheton pan kai osa peri to aistheton pathe e usteron ti touton kai os sumbebekos toutois e arkhe touton e en ti ton sumplerounton touto toiouton on ede gar an tis eis ennoian 0 PlutarchPericles apotetheien oi de dikastai ten psephon apo tou bomou pherontes en te polei krinoien agnon de touto men apheile tou psephismatos krinesthai de ten diken egrapsen en dikastais khiliois kai pentakosiois eite klopes kai doron eit adikiou bouloito tis onomazein ten dioxin aspasian men oun exetesato polla panu para ten diken os aiskhines phesin apheis uper autes dakrua kai deetheis ton dikaston anaxagoran de phobetheis exepempsen ek tes poleos os de dia pheidiou proseptaise to demo phobetheis to dikasterion mellonta ton polemon kai upotuphomenon exekausen elpizon diaskedasein ta egklemata kai tapeinosein ton phthonon en pragmasi megalois kai kindunois tes poleos ekeino mono dia to axioma kai ten dunamin anatheises eauten ai men oun aitiai di as ouk eiasen endounai lakedaimoniois ton demon autai legontai to d alethes adelon oi de lakedaimonioi ginoskontes os ekeinou kataluthentos eis panta malakoterois khresontai tois athenaiois ekeleuon autous to agos arkhidamon ekhonta tous peloponnesious proeipe tois athenaiois an ara talla deon o arkhidamos apekhetai ton ekeinou dia ten xenian ten ousan autois e diaboles tois ekhthrois endidous aphormas oti te all emeinen oikouron kai dia kheiros ekhon ten polin eos apellagesan oi peloponnesioi therapeuon de tous pollous omos askhallontas epi to polemo dianomais te khrematon anelambane kai kleroukhias egraphen aiginetas gar exelasas apantas dieneime ten neson athenaion tois lakhousin en de tis paregoria kai aph on epaskhon oi polemioi kai gar oi peripleontes ten peloponneson khoran te pollen komas genoito theoi timosin aoidous tis de ken allou akousai alis pantessin omeros outos aoidon lostos os ex emeu oisetai ouden daimonioi ti de kerdos o murios endothi khrusos keimenos oukh ade ploutou tetulomenos endothi kheiras akhen ek pateron penien aktemona klaion polloi en antiokhoio domois kai anaktos aleua armalien emmenon emetresanto penestai polloi de skopadesin elaunomenoi poti sakous 0 TheophrastusMetaphysics ten gen pleiosi tinos gar eneka ai ephodoi kai anarroiai thalattes e tinos ai prokhoreseis e anaxeranseis tes ugrotetos kai olos pros allot allo metabolai kai phthorai kai geneseis e ai men en aute te ge alloioseis kai metabolai gignontai pros allot allo methistamenon kai etera douk oliga paromoia toutois esti d en autois tois zoois ta men osper mataia kathaper tois arresin oi mastoi kai tois thelesin e proesis eiper me sumballetai kai pogonos d eniois e olos trikhon ekphusis en tisi topois eti de keraton megethe kathaper ton elaphon tois de kai lelobemenois kinesei te kai paraioresei kai epiprosthesei ton ommaton kai os enia de bia e para phnsin osper o erodios okheuei kai to emerobion ze kai etera ouk oliga laboi tis an toiauta kai to megnston de kai malista dokoun peri tas trophas kai geneseis ton zoon outhenos gar tauth eneka alla sumptomata kai di eteras anagkas edei gar eiper touton kharin aei kata tauta kai osautos eti den tois phutois kai mallon tois apsukhois orismenen tin ekhousi phusin osper dokousi kai morphais kai eidesi kai dunamesi tinos eneka tauta zeteseien an tis auto gar touto aporon to me ekhein logon kai taut en eterois me poiousi proterois kai timioterois e kai eoiken o logos ekhein ti piston os ara to automato tauta kai te tou olou periphora lambanei tinas ideas e pros allela diaphoras ei de me touth eneka tou kai eis to ariston lepteon tinas orous kai ouk epi panton aplos theteon epei kai ta toiade ekhei tina distasmon kai aplos legomen a kai kath ekaston aplos men oti ten phusin en apasin oregesthai tou aristou kai eph on endekhetai metadidonai tou aei kai tou tetagmenou os d autos kai epi ton zoon omoios opou gar oion te to beltion entautha oudamou paraleipei oion to emprosthen ten pharugga tou oisophagou timioteron gar kai en te mese koilia tes kardias ten krasin aristen oti to meson timiotaton osautos de kai osa kosmou kharin ei gar kai e orexis outos all ekeino g
0 Thucydides1 khorei autos de aph autou ta polla tekhnatai pros to paratugkhanon en o o men euorgetos auto prosomilesas bebaioteros o d orgistheis peri auton ouk elasso ptaiei enthumometha de kai oti ei men emon esan ekastois pros antipalous peri ges oron ai diaphorai oiston an en nun de pros xumpantas te emas athenaioi ikanoi kai kata polin eti dunatoteroi oste ei me kai athrooi kai kata ethne kai ekaston astu mia gnome amunoumetha autous dikha ge ontas emas aponos kheirosontai kai ten essan ei kai deinon to akousai isto ouk allo ti pherousan e antikrus douleian o kai logo endoiasthenai aiskhron te peloponneso kai poleis tosasde upo mias kakopathein en o e dikaios dokoimen an paskhein e dia deilian anekhesthai kai ton pateron kheirous phainesthai oi ten ellada eleutherosan emeis de oud emin autois bebaioumen auto turannon de eomen egkathestanai polin tous d en mia monarkhous axioumen kataluein kai ouk ismen opos tade trion ton megiston xumphoron apellaktai axunesias e malakias e ameleias ou gar de pepheugotes auta epi ten pleistous de blapsasan kataphronesin kekhorekate e ek tou pollous sphallein to enantion onoma aphrosune metonomastai ta men oun progegenemena ti dei makroteron e es oson tois nun xumpherei aitiasthai peri de ton epeita mellonton tois parousi boethountas khre epitalaiporein patrion gar umin ek ton ponon tas aretas ktasthai kai me metaballein to ethos ei ara plouto te nun kai exousia oligon propherete ou gar dikaion a te aporia ektethe te periousia apolesthai alla tharsountas ienai kata polla es ton polemon tou te theou khresantos kai autou uposkhomenou xullepsesthai kai tes alles ellados apases xunagonioumenes ta men phobo ta de ophelia spondas te ou lusete proteroi as ge kai o theos keleuon polemein nomizei parabebasthai edikemenais de mallon boethesete luousi gar oukh oi amunomenoi all oi proteroi epiontes oste pantakhothen kalos uparkhon umin polemein kai emon koine tade parainounton eiper bebaiotaton to tauta xumpheronta kai polesi kai idiotais einai me mellete poteideatais te poieisthai timorian ousi dorieusi kai upo ionon poliorkoumenois ou proteron en tounantion kai ton allon metelthein ten eleutherian os ouketi endekhetai perimenontas tous men ede blaptesthai tous d ei gnosthesometha xunelthontes men amunesthai de ou tolmontes me polu usteron to auto paskhein alla nomisantes es anagken aphikhthai o andres xummakhoi kai ama tade arista legesthai psephisasthe ton polemon me phobethentes to autika deinon tes d ap autou dia pleionos eirenes epithumesantes ek polemou men gar eirene mallon bebaioutai aph esukhias de me polemesai oukh omoios akindunon kai ten kathestekuian en te elladi polin turannon egesamenoi epi pasin omoios kathestanai oste ton men ede arkhein ton de dianoeisthaiparastesometha epelthontes kai autoi te akindunos to loipon oikomen kai tous nun dedoulomenous ellenas eleutherosomen toiauta men oi korinthioi eipon oi de lakedaimonioi epeide aph apanton ekousan gnomen psephon epegagon tois xummakhois apasin osoi paresan exes kai meizoni kai elassoni polei kai to plethos epsephisanto polemein dedogmenon de autois euthus men adunata en epikheirein aparaskeuois ousin ekporizesthai de edokei ekastois a prosphora en kai me einai mellesin omos de kathistamenois on edei eniautos men ou dietribe elasson de prin esbalein es ten attiken kai ton polemon arasthai phaneros en touto de epresbeuonto to khrono pros tous athenaious egklemata poioumenoi opos sphisin oti megiste prophasis eie tou polemein en me ti esakouosin kai proton men presbeis pempsantes oi lakedaimonioi ekeleuon tous athenaious to agos elaunein tes theou to de agos en toionde kulon en athenaios aner olumpionikes ton palai eugenes te kai dunatos egegamekei de thugatera theagenous megareos andros os kat ekeinon ton khronon eturannei megaron khromeno de to kuloni en delphois aneilen o theos en tou dios te megiste eorte katalabein ten athenaion akropolin o de para te tou theagenous dunamin labon kai tous philous anapeisas epeide epelthen olumpia ta en peloponneso katelabe ten akropolin os epi turannidi nomisas eorten te tou dios megisten einai kai eauto ti prosekein olumpia nenikekoti ei de en te attike e allothi pou e megiste eorte eireto oute ekeinos eti katenoese to te manteion ouk edelou esti gar kai athenaiois diasia a kaleitai dios eorte meilikhiou megiste exo tes poleos en e pandemei thuousi polla oukh iereia all agna thumata epikhoria dokon de orthos gignoskein epekheirese to ergo oi de athenaioi aisthomenoi eboethesan te pandemei ek ton agron ep autous kai proskathezomenoi epoliorkoun khronou de eggignomenou oi athenaioi trukhomenoi te prosedria apelthon oi polloi epitrepsantes tois ennea arkhousi ten te phulaken kai to pan autokratorsi diatheinai e an arista diagignoskosin tote de ta polla ton politikon oi ennea arkhontes eprasson oi de meta tou kulonos poliorkoumenoi phlauros eikhon sitou te kai udatos aporia o men oun kulon kai o adelphos autou ekdidraskousin oi d alloi os epiezonto kai tines kai apethneskon upo tou limou kathizousin epi ton bomon iketai ton en te akropolei anastesantes de autous oi ton athenaion epitetrammenoi ten phulaken os eoron apothneskontas en to iero eph o meden kakon poiesousin apagagontes apekteinan kathezomenous de tinas kai epi ton semnon theon tois bomois en te parodo apekhresanto kai apo toutou enageis kai aliterioi tes theou ekeinoi te ekalounto kai to genos to ap ekeinon elasan men oun kai oi athenaioi tous enageis toutous elase de kai kleomenes o lakedaimonios usteron meta athenaion stasiazonton tous te zontas elaunontes kai ton tethneoton ta osta anelontes exebalon katelthon mentoi usteron kai to genos auton estin eti en te polei touto de to agos oi lakedaimonioi ekeleuon elaunein dethen tois theois proton timorountes eidotes de periklea ton ksanthippou prosekhomenon auto kata ten metera kai nomizontes ekpesontos autou raon an sphisi prokhorein ta apo ton athenaion ou mentoi tosouton elpizon pathein an auton touto oson diabolen oisein auto pros ten polin os kai dia ten ekeinou xumphoran to meros estai o polemos on gar dunatotatos ton kath eauton kai agon ten politeian enantiouto panta tois lakedaimoniois kai ouk eia upeikein all es ton polemon orma tous athenaious antekeleuon de kai oi athenaioi tous lakedaimonious to apo tainarou agos elaunein oi gar lakedaimonioi anastesantes pote ek tou ierou tou poseidonos apo tainarou ton eiloton iketas apagagontes diephtheiran di o de kai sphisin autois nomizousi ton megan seismon genesthai en sparte ekeleuon de kai to tes khalkioikou agos elaunein autous egeneto de toionde epeide pausanias o lakedaimonios to proton metapemphtheis upo spartiaton apo tes arkhes tes en ellesponto kai kritheis up auton apeluthe me adikein demosia men ouketi exepemphthe idia de autos triere labon ermionida aneu lakedaimonion aphikneitai es ellesponton to men logo epi ton ellenikon polemon to de ergo ta pros basilea pragmata prassein osper kai to proton epekheiresen ephiemenos tes ellenikes arkhes euergesian de apo toude proton es basilea katetheto kai tou pantos pragmatos arkhen epoiesato buzantion gar elon te protera parousia meta ten ek kuprou anakhoresin eikhon de medoi auto kai basileos prosekontes tines kai xuggeneis oi ealosan en auto tote toutous ous elaben apopempei basilei krupha ton allon xummakhon to de logo apedrasan auton eprasse de tauta meta goggulou tou eretrios oper epetrepse to te buzantion kai tous aikhmalotous epempse de kai epistolen ton goggulon pheronta auto enegegrapto de tade en aute os usteron aneurethe pausanias o egemon tes spartes tousde te soi kharizesthai boulomenos apopempei dori elonkai gnomen poioumai ei kai soi dokei thugatera te ten sen gemai kai soi sparten te kai ten allen ellada upokheirion poiesai dunatos de doko einai tauta praxai meta sou bouleuomenos ei oun ti se touton areskei pempe andra piston epi thalassan di ou to loipon tous logous poiesometha tosauta men e graphe edelou kserxes de esthe te te epistole kai apostellei artabazon ton pharnakou epi thalassan kai keleuei auton ten te daskulitin satrapeian paralabein megabaten apallaxanta os proteron erkhe kai para pausanian es buzantion epistolen antepetithei auto os takhista diapempsai kai ten sphragida apodeixai kai en ti auto pausanias paraggelle peri ton eautou pragmaton prassein os arista kai pistotata o de aphikomenos ta te alla epoiesen osper eireto kai ten epistolen diepempsen antenegegrapto de tade ode legei basileus kserxes pausania kai ton andron ous moi peran thalasses ek buzantiou esosas keisetai soi euergesia en to emetero oiko es aiei anagraptos kai tois logois tois apo sou areskomai kai se mete nux meth emera episkheto oste aneinai prassein ti on emoi upiskhne mede khrusou kai argurou dapane kekolustho mede stratias plethei ei poi dei paragignesthai alla met artabazou andros agathou on soi epempsa prasse tharson kai ta ema kai ta sa ope kallista kai arista exei bioteuein alla skeuas te medikas enduomenos ek tou buzantiou exeei kai dia tes thrakes poreuomenon auton medoi kai aiguptioi edoruphoroun trapezan te persiken paretitheto kai katekhein ten dianoian keleusanton auton toiauta ephaineto poion kai ek tou buzantiou bia up athenaion ekpoliorketheis es men ten sparten ouk epanekhorei es de kolonas tas troadas idrutheis prasson te eseggelleto autois es 0 Xenocrates ksenokrates agathenoros khalkedonios a ten monada kai ten duada theous ten men os patros ekhousan taxin en ourano basileuousan entina prosagoreuei kai zena kai peritton kai noun ostis kai puthagoras kai ksenokrates kai khrusippos epomenoi tois palai theologois men anthropon gegonenai legousi kai polle te dunamei ten phusin uperpherontas emon to de theion ouk amiges oud akraton kai platon kai ksenokrates kai khrusippos o de ksenokrates kai ton emeron tas apophradas kai ton eorton osai plegas tinas e kopetous e nesteias e dusphemias e aiskhrologian ekhousin oute theon timais oute daimonon oietai prosekein khreston alla einai phuseis en to periekhonti megalas men kai iskhuras dustropous de kai skuthropas ai khairousi tois toioutois kai tugkhanousai pros outhen allo kheiron trepontai o de ksenokrates ta men astra kai ton elion ek puros phesi kai tou protou puknou sugkeisthai ten de selenen ek tou deuterou puknou kai tou idiou aeros ten de gen ex udatos kai puros kai tou tritou ton puknon olos de mete to puknon auto kath auto mete to manon einai psukhes dektikon ksenokrates kata mian epiphaneian oietai keisthai sthai tous asteras oi de alloi stoikoi pro ton eteron ron tous eterous en upsei kai bathei kai gar auton outo ton kosmon ek ton ano kai ton kato phusei pheromenon sunermosmenon apellakhthai pantapasi tes kata topon kineseos tauta de kai ksenokrates eoiken ennoesai theio tini logismo ten arkhen labon para platonos ksenokrates metron ton genneton kai kinesin ton khronon elege dokei men pros ksenokraten malista kai tous platonikous o logos teinein dioti ex ataktou kai plemmelous gegonenai ton kosmon phasi tou platonos eipontos paralabon gar o theos pan oson en oraton oukh esukhian agon alla kinoumenon plemmelos kai ataktos eis taxin auto egagen ek kai sunthetoteron empedokles kai ksenokrates ek mikroteron ogkon ta stoikheia sugkrinei aper estin elakhista kai oionei stoikheia stoikheion ksenokrates kai diodoros amere ta elakhista orizonto ti oun oukhi kai platoni sunebaine kai aristotelei kai ksenokratei khruson ek me khrusou kai lithon ek me lithou kai talla gennan ek tessaron aplon kai proton apanton panu men oun all ekeinois men euthus te suniasin ai arkhai pros ten ekastou genesin osper sumbolas megalas pherousai tas en autais poiotetas kai otan sunelthosin eis to auto kai sumpesosi xerois ugra kai psukhra thermois kai sterea malthakois somata kinoumena pathetikois ap allelon kai metaballonta di olon eteran aph eteras kraseos sunapotiktei genesin oi de peri ksenokraten ten men proten akolouthian upeinai sunekhoroun tout estin oti ei en esti to on kai adiaireton estai ou men adiaireton einai to on dio palin mede en monon to on alla pleio diaireton mentoi me ep apeiron einai all eis atoma tina katalegein tauta mentoi me atoma einai os amere kai elakhista alla to poson kai ten ulen tmeta kai mere ekhonta to de eidei atoma kai prota protas tinas upotithemenos einai grammas atomous kai ta ek touton epipeda kai sterea prota ten oun ek tes dikhotomias kai aplos tes ep apeiron tomes kai diaireseos upantosan aporian o ksenokrates oietai dialuesthai tas atomous eisagagon grammas kai aplos atoma poiesas megethe pheugon to on eiper esti diaireton eis to me on analuthenai kai analothenai ton atomon grammon ex on upistatai ta onta atmeton menouson kai adiaireton epei de kai ksenokrates sophos en aner pos ara tas atomous grammas upetitheto oude gar egnoei ten phusin tou megethous all oude to eidei adiaireton elege touto gar ou monon ai elakhistai grammai ekhousin alla kai ta megista somata mepote oun ou pros ten ep apeiron tomen enistato o ksenokrates ou gar an geometriken arkhen aneilen geometrikos on aner alla pros to eis apeira dieresthai onton aei tinon atmeton megethon atina oude upo phuseos iskhuei kath auta diaireisthai dia smikroteta all enothenta palin allois somasin outo tou olou diairoumenou en eautois ekeinen dekhetai ten diairesin en mona onta ouk an upemeinen os oun o platon epipeda eipen einai ta prota kai elakhista somata outos o ksenokrates grammas adiairetous men dia smikroteta diairetas de kai autas ousas te phusei alla men dedeiktai en te phusike akroasei en tois peri kikeseos logois en ois antelege pros ksenokraten grammas atomous legonta oti ouk eisin adiairetoi grammai tout estin oti ouden meros grammes estin adiaireton all eis apeiron esti diaireton ouk ara ek semeion esti gramme oud ek grammon to epipedon oud ex epipedon to stereon tauta men ta aristotelous oper aei ephen apantontos pros to tou logou phainomenon reteon de oti eiper ta epipeda elegon mathematika einai os mekos monon kai platos ekhein oi ex epipedon ta sterea legontes kai eis ta epipeda auta analuontes kalos o aristoteles kai tauta autois epegage ta atopa kai ta exes epaxei ei de phusika ta epipeda legousin os me monon mekos kai platos alla kai bathos ekhein oper arkhen en tois phusikois kathistanai dunaton ouketi te thesei auton epetai ta atopa ta epagomena pros ta epipeda os me bebathusmena oti de phusika kai ou mathematika ta epipeda upotithentai delon ek tou enula legein auta dio kai ten ulen proteron paradontes dieskhematisthai tauten eidesi te kai arithmois legousi kai autos de o timaios en to oikeio suggrammati tade gegraphen arkhai men on ton gennomenon ktl ei d estin adiaireta megethe kai apathe kai khoris poiotetos os oi peri demokriton elegon kai ksenokrates atomous grammas upotithemenos ex enantias tois mathematikois an aphomoiointo ksenokrates men pros ten ep apeiron tomen tas atomous grammas eisagei ina pheuge tauton en te kai polla legein en antiphasin kakos upolambanon etera periepipten antiphasei khalepotera tauton ama poion megethos te kai ou megethos kaitoi tauton men en te kai polla legein ouk estin antikeimena ei diairoito tis to dunamei kai energeia tauton de poiein grammen te kai adiaireton antikrus esti poiountos ten grammen ou grammen enthen o ksenokrates anerei ten ep apeiron ton megethon tomen autos goun pollakhos sugkhoresas touto alethei onti omos epelusato monakhos ten aporian en ois kai touto phesin oti ton megethon e tome dunamei men estin ep apeiron energeia d ou adunaton gar energeia genesthai to apeiron oste kai e kinesis dunamei men di apeiron eleusetai energeia de dia peperasmenon oude gar kata semeion ginetai e kinesis alla kata megethos orismenon dikhotomian de ekalese ten zenonos epikheiresin kai delon dia ti dioti to lephthen megethos dikha temnein outos epoieito ten kataskeuen eipomen de kai en to proto logo oti tines ton ksenokraten upopteusan tas atomous eisegeisthai grammas kai edeixamen os pseudes e uponoia elegkhoito d an dia tou problematos toutou kai o ksenokrateios logos o tas atomous eisagon grammas olos gar ei esti gramme e eutheia esti kai dunaton auten dikha temein e peripheres kai meizon estin eutheias tinos pasa gar peripheres pantos ekhei tina eutheian elassona e mikte kai pollo pleon aute diairete estin eiper ex aplon esti diaireton alla tauta men eis allen anabeblestho theorian psukhe arithmos eauton kinon epei de ton dokimotaton andron tous men ksenokrates prosegageto tes psukhes ten ousian arithmon auton uph eautou kinoumenon apophenamenos oi men gar ouden allo e genesin arithmou delousthai nomizousi te mixei tes ameristou kai meristes ousias ameriston men gar einai to en meriston de to plethos ek de touton ginesthai ton arithmon tou enos orizontos to plethos kai te apeiria peras entithentos en kai duada kalousin aoriston touton de mepo psukhen ton arithmon einai to gar kinetikon kai to kineton endein auto tou de tautou kai tou eterou summigenton on to men esti kineseos arkhe kai metaboles to de mones psukhen gegonenai meden etton tou istanai kai istasthai dunamin e tou kineisthai kai kinein ousan puthagoras ten psukhen apephenato arithmon auton kinounta ton d arithmon anti tou nou paralambanei omoios de kai ksenokrates b esan de eteroi oi kai ta duo ama sumplekontes eis ten apodosin tes psukhes to te kinein kai to gignoskein os o ten psukhen apophenamenos arithmon kinounta eauton dia men tou arithmou ten gnostiken dunamin endeiknumenos dia de tou kinein eauton ten kinetiken puthagoras de sumbolikos eikazein aei kai ton theon kai panta tois arithmois eiothos orisato kai ten psukhen arithmon eauton kinounta o kai ksenokrates ekolouthesen oukh oti arithmos estin e psukhe all oti en tois arithmetois esti kai en tois peplethusmenois kai oti e psukhe estin e diakrinousa ta pragmata to morphas kai tupous ekastois epiballein aute gar estin e ta eide apo ton eidon khorizousa kai diaphora auta apophainousa te te eteroteti ton eidon kai to plethei tou arithmou kai dia touto arithmeta poiousa ta pragmata othen ou pantapasin apellaktai tes kata tous arithmous koinonias ksenokrates arithmon auten ten psukhen themenos en poso dokei ksenokratous o tes psukhes outos logos boulomenou ten mesoteta autes ton te eidon kai ton eidopoioumenon ama kai to idion autes endeixasthai o gar arithmos to eidos to de kineton tois eidopoioumenois prosekei ek men sun ton akron monon ou deloi to oute arithmos aplos estai oute kinetos tou men gar upheitai e tou ameristou ekbebletai tou de esti kreisson e tou meristou uperekhei to sunamphoteron oun an pos eie os amphoterois koinonousa arithmos kinetos kata de to oikeion tes mesotetos uph eautou kinetos legetai oti oukh os diastatike esti mese e psukhe oios o phusikos logos kai pro toutou kata tous andras e mathematike ousia oude oia kata to proion apo nou phos ousia noera a men eti menousa to de eis to phanon kai summetron tois upo nou katalampomenois proerkhesthai diaggellousa to monimon kai kruphion tes noeras b phuseos alla kat auten ten zotiken idioteta egersin kai zesin tina pases delouses zoes ameriston men kai en eaute menousan tes noeras peri de ta somata merizomenen kai eterothen eis etera uphizanousan tes somatoeidous tes de psukhes ten aph eautes eis anelixin kai eis diastasin ama sunagogen dia tauta men oun o ksenokrates arithmon auton eauton kinounta ten psukhen apephenato o de aristoteles ton arithmon oristikon proeipon kai ton gnoston kai ton gnostikon epi tes psukhes eulogos os gnostikon eiresthai akouei kai dia touto tous eipontas ten psukhen arithmon auton eauton kinounta sumplexai ephe to kinetikon kai to gnostikon oi de upo to poson on esti kai ksenokrates arithmos gar phesi kinon eauton estin e psukhe o de arithmos upo to poson ei de touto elegen ekeinos kai me allo ti dia toutou enitteto epi tauto de pherontai kai osoi legousi ten psukhen to auto kinoun eoikasi gar outoi pantes upeilephenai ten kinesin oikeiotaton einai te psukhe kai ta men alla panta kineisthai dia ten psukhen tauten d uph eautes dia to methen oran kinoun o me kai auto kineitai ksenokrates o toutou diadokhos ap amphoteron orizetai ten psukhen eipon auten arithmon kinounta eauton dia men to gnostiken einai auten ton onton arithmon eipon os puthagoras arkhe gar panton arithmos kata autous dia de to kinetiken einai to autokineton anatheis aute arkhe gar kai pege pases kineseos kat autous to autokineton ksenokrates elegen oun arithmon men ten psukhen dia to pleroma eidon einai ten psukhen kai logon ek ton logon panton gar en eaute tous logous ekhei os eipomen arithmous de ta eide ekaloun os eiretai kai autos goun en tois exes phesin kai eu de oi legontes ten psukhen topon eidon arithmon men oun dia touto kinounta de auton dia to autozon autes ou gar uph eterou aute to zen autozoe gar estin toioutos de kai o tes psukhes oros ei arithmos autos auton kinon esti kai gar to auto auto kinoun psukhe kathaper platon oristai osper psukhes orismos to arithmos autos eauton kinon to gar arithmos ek perittou keitai kai gar to auto eauto kinoun khoris tou arithmou ten psukhen deloi kathaper platon en to phaidro phesi legon athanatou de pephasmenou tou uph eautou kinoumenou psukhes ousian te kai logon touto tis legon ouk aiskhuneitai allos te kai o arithmos ouk esti genos tes psukhes osper de tinos enistamenou kai legontos pos phes oti aphairethentos tou arithmou ou lumainetai o orismos genos gar esti tes psukhes o arithmos kata ksenokraten kai platona kai dei tes prosthekes tou arithmou os genous en to orismo phesin oti ei dosomen oti o arithmos genos esti tes psukhes aphairethentos toutou to kataleiphthen ouk estai oros all idion ou men de kai ten ousian delosei tou pragmatos pas men gar oros idion ou men kai to anapalin opoteros men oun ekhei omos khalepon esti diasaphenisai opoteron genos psukhes o arithmos e ou kai poteron aphairethentos tou arithmou to kataleipomenon orismos esti tes psukhes e idion e ou meizonos gar skepseos e peri touto zetesis e tes dialektikes eipe oun ei o arithmos o ksenokrates e perittos estin e artios e psukhe e artios estin e perittos kai ei artios e tettares estin e st ei de perittos a e e e z e oun psukhe ti esti d e e kai epei ek pantos arithmou ekballomenes monados eteros arithmos kataleipetai oion apo tou st o e kai apo b tou z palin o st tina arithmon apo apodotheis orismos arithmos gar phesin esti kinon eauton o gar touton akousas ouden eikasai kai labein ex autou ton te psukhe e to zoo uparkhonton dunesetai polu de ton eiremenon alogoteron to legein arithmon einai ten psukhen kinounth eauton uparkhei gar autois adunata prota men ta ek tou kineisthai sumbainonta idia de ek tou legein auten arithmon meta de tauta dielegkhei ton ksenokratous orismon
